***perspectief.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:perspectief.html>perspectief</a> (9228)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From Old <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span>, from the first word of the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">perspectiva ars</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">science of optics</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the feminine of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">perspectivus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">of sight, optical</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">perspectus</i>, the past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">perspicere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to inspect, look through</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">per-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">through</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">specere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to look at</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; the noun sense <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> influenced or mediated by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">prospettiva</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">prospetto</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">prospect</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:perspectief.html>perspectief</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:perspectieven.html>perspectieven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:perspectief.html>perspectiefje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

***persuasion.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> persuasion (8467)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b>persuasion</b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:overtuiging.html>overtuiging</a>
<dl><dd>«I am not of your <b>persuasion</b>.»
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>uw</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:overtuiging.html>overtuiging</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>overtuigingskracht, overredingskracht
<dl><dd>«It <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> a lot of <b>persuasion</b> to convince the committee of the advantages of the new scheme.»

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:perzik.html>perzik</a> (13630)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">perseke</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">persicum</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">persica</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>

***pesto.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pesto.html>pesto</a> (44860)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1937, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:pesto.html>pesto</a></i>, contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">pestato</i>, form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">pestare</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pound in a mortar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pestle</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pesto.html>pesto</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pestos</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A sauce, especially for <a href = vnd.unilang:pasta.html>pasta</a>, originating from the Genoa region in Italy, made from <a href = vnd.unilang:basil.html>basil</a>, garlic, pine <a href = vnd.unilang:nuts.html>nuts</a>, olive oil and cheese (usually pecorino)</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pesto.html>pesto</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:voeding.html>voeding</a>)</span> Italiaanse basilicumsaus
<dl><dd><ul><li><i> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunt.html>kunt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pesto.html>pesto</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meeste.html>meeste</a> Italiaanse <a href = vnd.unilang:gerechten.html>gerechten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebruiken.html>gebruiken</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

***peul.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:peul.html>peul</a> (48691)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pole</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:peul.html>peul</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:peulen.html>peulen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:peultje.html>peultje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>pea pod, bean pod</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">especially in the diminutive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> snow pea, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Pisum_sativum_var._saccharatum" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Pisum sativum var. saccharatum"><i>Pisum <a href = vnd.unilang:sativum.html>sativum</a></i> var. <i>saccharatum</i></a></span>, or its pod eaten as food</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">peulschil</span></li></ul>

***pezen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pezen.html>pezen</a> (32390)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pees.html>pees</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sinew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">pesen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pezen.html>pezen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run or walk <span class="Latn" lang="en">quickly</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to work with <span class="Latn" lang="en">considerable</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">effort</span></li>

<p>The term derives from African American Vernacular English as a deliberate misspelling of the word <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fat</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:piccalilly.html>piccalilly</a> (73559)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">piccalilli</i>.

***piek.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:piek.html>piek</a> (7999)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pike</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:piek.html>piek</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pieken.html>pieken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:piek.html>piekje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A highest point; a peak.</li>
<li>A summit, a peak, the highest point of a mountain.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bergtop.html>bergtop</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">top</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A pike <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">polearm</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:guilder.html>guilder</a> (<i>comparable to buck, quid</i>).</li>
<li>A spire tree-topper for a Christmas tree.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">peak</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">piekbui</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">piekervaring</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">piekuur</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">pike</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">piekenier</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:guilder.html>guilder</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">piekenpijp</span></li></ul>

***pieken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pieken.html>pieken</a> (20987)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">pic</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sharp point or spike</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">picus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">woodpecker</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) and/or <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">pique</i>, its descendant <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">piquer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pick, sting, stab</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>); the verb may, in some senses, derive from cognate synonym <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pikken.html>pikken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pick, hack</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pieken.html>pieken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:piek.html>piek</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pieken.html>pieken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reach a peak, culminate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to climax, (have) reach(ed) the peak (level) etc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pick, hack, hit and affect with a pointy instrument, especially a pickaxe</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stick, pin, with a sharp object which may penetrate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sting, hurt</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stick out</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">pick</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pikken.html>pikken</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sting</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijten.html>bijten</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steken.html>steken</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pieken.html>pieken</a></b>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:piemel.html>piemel</a> (12987)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">piemelen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pee, water</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Pimmel</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:piemel.html>piemel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:piemels.html>piemels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:piemeltje.html>piemeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:pecker.html>pecker</a>, cock, <a href = vnd.unilang:dick.html>dick</a>, euphemism for <a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fluit.html>fluit</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leuter.html>leuter</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lul.html>lul</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pik.html>pik</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snikkel.html>snikkel</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">tampeloeris</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dude, guy

<li>urine
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pis.html>pis</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plas.html>plas</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">urine</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">water</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeik.html>zeik</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
